<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:muts.html>muts</a> (8567)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mutse</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Mütze</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muts.html>muts</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mutsen.html>mutsen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mutsje.html>mutsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>tuque (knitted winter cap), a type of brimless hat; a similar soft (nearly) brimless hat
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:muts.html>muts</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoofd.html>hoofd</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kraag.html>kraag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:staat.html>staat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:omhoog.html>omhoog</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ijskoud.html>ijskoud</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkig.html>gelukkig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:droog.html>droog</a>.</i><small>(Guus Meeuwis  |  Brabant)</small>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:muur.html>muur</a> (1080)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:muur.html>muur</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mure</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*mūr</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*mūra</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mūrus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muur.html>muur</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muren.html>muren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:muur.html>muurtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A wall.</li>
<li>A type of <a href = vnd.unilang:fast-food.html>fast-food</a> vending machine with compartments arranged similar to a wall that contain <a href = vnd.unilang:snacks.html>snacks</a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">chiefly in the phrase "<a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:muur.html>muur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:trekken.html>trekken</a>"</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mythe.html>mythe</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-logie</i>. lang="la">mythologia</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μυθολογία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">muthología</span>, <span from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μυθολόγος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">muthológos</span>, <span ***na.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a> (203)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*nāh</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*nā</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*nēhw</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_2">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>after</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> ... <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a></span><span class="ib-comma">,</span> with a cardinal number</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:bar.html>bar</a>, except <span class="use-with-mention">Used to form ordinal numbers in relation to a superlative quality. The number that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> 1 lower than in the English translation.</span>
<dl><dd><i>Brazilië <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> 8,5 <a href = vnd.unilang:miljoen.html>miljoen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vierkant.html>vierkante</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kilometer.html>kilometer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grootste.html>grootste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Zuid-Amerika <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vier.html>vier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grootste.html>grootste</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ter.html>ter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wereld.html>wereld</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>With its 8.5 million square <a href = vnd.unilang:kilometers.html>kilometers</a>, Brazil <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the largest country in South America and the <b>fifth largest</b> in the world.</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:naast.html>Naast</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toonladder.html>toonladder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kenmerkend.html>kenmerkend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gegeven.html>gegeven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bepaalde.html>bepaalde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tonen.html>tonen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:speciale.html>speciale</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rol.html>rol</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zoals.html>zoals</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> vadi <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> samvadi, <a href = vnd.unilang:respectievelijk.html>respectievelijk</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:belangrijkste.html>belangrijkste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:belangrijkste.html>belangrijkste</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:toon.html>toon</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>Next to [the fact] that the musical scale <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a characteristic datum, there are also certain tones that have a special role, such as the vadi and the samvadi: respectively the most important and <i>second most important</i> tones.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*nāh</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*nā</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*nēhwaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nader.html>nader</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naast.html>naast</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>close</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection_2">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The forms of the positive are obsolescent, particularly the inflected one. The comparative and superlative forms are functioning as independent adjectives to an increasing extent.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:naad.html>naad</a> (16071)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">naet</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*nād</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*nēdiz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">seam</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>A seam, as where pieces of textile are sewn together</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Another <span class="Latn" lang="en">joint</span> or <span class="Latn" lang="en">juncture</span>, notably in construction, <a href = vnd.unilang:mechanics.html>mechanics</a>, etc.</li>

***naakt.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:naakt.html>naakt</a> (1992)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">naket</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">naect</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">nakot</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*nakwadaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*nogʷós</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">naked, bare</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">naakd</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">nackt</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">naked</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">neaken</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">nøgen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">naken</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naakt.html>naakt</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naakt.html>naakter</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">naaktst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>nude, not wearing any clothing; can also apply to part of the body with exposed hide</li>
<li>naked, bald, without protective fur, <a href = vnd.unilang:feathers.html>feathers</a> etc. on the skin</li>
<li>bare, stripped, reduced to its essence
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfs.html>Zelfs</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:naakte.html>naakte</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:waarheid.html>waarheid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verslaan.html>verslaan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:naakte.html>naakte</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:cijfer.html>cijfers</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:opgeven.html>opgeven</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:naakte.html>naakte</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:feiten.html>feiten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vaak.html>vaak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:betekenis.html>betekenis</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:samenhang.html>samenhang</a></i>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>Even</a> covering the naked truth <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> more than listing the naked figures: the naked <a href = vnd.unilang:facts.html>facts</a> often only have meaning in context</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:naakte.html>naakte</a> (5531)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Germanic, cognate with naked, German nackt
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naakte.html>naakte</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naakten.html>naakten</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>naked person
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>Onder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haveloze.html>haveloze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vluchtelingen.html>vluchtelingen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zelfs.html>zelfs</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enkele.html>enkele</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:naakten.html>naakten</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>Among the destitute refugees <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> some <b>nude <a href = vnd.unilang:ones.html>ones</a></b>.</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:naakten.html>naakten</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:kleden.html>kleden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> één <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>werken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:barmhartigheid.html>barmhartigheid</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>Clothing the <b>nude</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> one of the charitable <a href = vnd.unilang:acts.html>acts</a>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naakte.html>naakte</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Inflected form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naakt.html>naakt</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naakte.html>naakte</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention"> singular past indicative and subjunctive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">naken</i></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:naakte.html>naakte</a></b>
</p>

<ol><li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:nudist.html>nudist</a> beach, a nude beach; a beach where one <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> allowed or required to practice nudism.</li></ol>

***naald.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:naald.html>naald</a> (5346)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">naelde</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">nālda</i>, from a metathesis of earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*nādla</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*nēþlō</i>. Compare the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> alternative form <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">nālda</i>, whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Luxembourgish" class="extiw" title="w:Luxembourgish">Luxembourgish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lb">Nol</i>. Also cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Nadel</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">needle</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naald.html>naald</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naalden.html>naalden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naald.html>naaldje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A needle, a pin <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">for sewing, injections, tattooing etc.</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li>A needle <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">leaf of coniferous trees</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li>The needle of a record player.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">architecture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:obelisk.html>obelisk</a> or column <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">monument, memorial</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naald.html>naald</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">needle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hak.html>hak</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">name</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">namo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*namô</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁nómn̥</i>. ***naar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> (34)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*nār</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*nēhwiz</i>. Originally the comparative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a></i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> in Modern Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nader.html>nader</a></i>. Compare also English: <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">near</i>, Swedish: <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">när</i> and Danish and Norwegian <i>når</i>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to, towards in time, space, consequence, purpose etc.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>according</a> to, in accordance with
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:evangelie.html>Evangelie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:judas.html>Judas</a></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>according</a> to the gospel of <a href = vnd.unilang:judas.html>Judas</a></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<div class="NavFrame" style="width: 30em;">
<div class="NavHead" style="background: CCCCFF; text-align: left;">Pronominal adverbs of <i lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a></i></div>
<div class="NavContent">

</div>
</div>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">naer</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:nare.html>nare</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tight, sad</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*naro</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">narrow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*narwaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">narrow, tight, constricted</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)ner-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">turn, bend, twist, constrict</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ghastly, dismal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">near</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">narrow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">narrow</i>; compare also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Narbe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">scar, closed wound</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">narrow</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naarder</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">naarst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>nasty, scary</li>
<li>unpleasant, sickening</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geest.html>geest</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:naarstig.html>naarstig</a> (68568)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">nernstich</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">nernst</i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">-ich</i>, with <i>nernst</i> a variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ernst.html>ernst</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">seriousness; industry, diligence</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">naarst</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>

<ol><li>assiduous, diligent, industrious</li></ol>

***naatje.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:naatje.html>naatje</a> (43365)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naatje.html>Naatje</a></i>, a nickname of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nl:Naatje_van_de_Dam" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:nl:Naatje van de Dam"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> Monument <a href = vnd.unilang:ter.html>ter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:herinnering.html>herinnering</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> den Hollandse Volkswil</a>, possibly influenced by <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naadje.html>naadje</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:vulva.html>vulva</a>, slit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, though <i><a href = vnd.unilang:naatje.html>Naatje</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> already in use as a (<a href = vnd.unilang:nick.html>nick</a>)name for women at the time. The statue <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> of poor quality.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naatje.html>naatje</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> only used as part of a predicate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Something that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> of poor quality or that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unpleasant; something that <a href = vnd.unilang:sucks.html>sucks</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:naatje.html>naatje</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moeten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vertrekken.html>vertrekken</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">It <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sucks.html>sucks</a> hard</b> that they have to already leave now.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nieuwe.html>nieuwe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boek.html>boek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:echt.html>echt</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:naatje.html>naatje</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>'s new book really <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sucks.html>sucks</a></b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
